class="text_exposed_root"&gt;&lt;p&gt;This Artist&#039;s Hyperrealistic Wood Sculptures Are Basically Human &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt; The Huffington Post | Dominique Mosbergen:&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt; Bruno Walpoth can practically turn wood into flesh.&lt;span class="text_exposed_hide"&gt;...&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class="text_exposed_show"&gt; The Italian artist has a knack for creating haunting, incredibly lifelike sculptures hewn out of wood.
